N63 ; Axis          C :0.

N821 ;TOOL ASSEMBLY     = SFSL_D20.0_LG

N822 ;(---------------------------------------------)

N823 MSG(" MO : 5X_SIMUL_ROUGHING ")

N824 ;(---------------------------------------------)

N825 TRAORI(1)

N826 D1

N827 G00 X-30.768 Y66.754 Z100 A-0.17 C-201.93

 

4     Programming Modes

 

The PP supports two different 5X-Programming-Modes

  • 5-X Simultaneous Mode
  • Plane-Mode (àSiemens FRAME )

 

The corresponding 5X-Mode will be activated with the PP-Word PROGMODE

 

5-X Simultaneous

PROGMODE/5XSIM

 

Plane

PROGMODE/FRAME

 

 

Standard: PROGMODE/FRAME ist activated.

 

4.1     5-X Simulteous Mode

 

This Mode is used fort he 5X-Simultaneous-Machining. One NC-Sentence contain X-, Y-, Z-Coordinates and the two
Rotation Angles A and C. The Data corresponds to the NC-Axis-System.

Application:

  • 5-X Simultaneous Machining
  • 5-X Drilling without Cycles (for example normal to the Surface)

Limits:

  • No Circle Output. If there are Circles into APT-File, these Circles will be linarised by the PP.
  • 2D Cuttercompensation not supportet.

PP-Output: ToolTip-Coordinates.

 

4.2     Plane Mode

This Mode is used for prismatic Machining on Planes not perpendicular to the axis system (Slope).  If Plane-Mode
is activated, the PP recognize automatic new Planes and set the internal SETPLN-Sequence. So the new Plane
will be activated automatically.

Supported in Plane-Mode:

  • Circles
  • 2D Cuttercompensation
  • Drilling-Cycles

 

4.3     Manipulation of the Angle-Calculation


Two Variants are possible fort he Manipulation of the Angle-Calculation (Rotaxis)

In most cases, ANGTWO and SETANG hase similar effects.

4.3.1     ANGTWO

Syntax:            ANGTWO

Normaly there are more then one Angle-Solution to receive a specific Vector-Position. The PP calculates the shortest Way from the actual position.



If the programmer prefers the second Solution, he can use the PP-Word ANGTWO.


Vector

Basis-Angle

1. Solution

ANGTWO Solution

0.866025,
0.433013,
0.250000

A0 C0


A-60 C60

 

A-120 C-120

 

4.3.2     SETANG

Syntax:            SETANG/<a>, <b>, <c>


With the command SETANG the programmer has influence into the „PP-internal“ Angle-Position.

 

Vector

„Angle-Position“ befor SETANG

SETANG

„Angle-Position“ after SETANG

calculated Angle-Solution

0.866025,
0.433013,
0.250000

A0 C0

SETANG/0,0,0

A0 C0

A-60 C60

A0 C0

SETANG/0,150,0

A0 C150

A120 C120

A0 C0

SETANG/200,0,0

A200 C0

A300 C60

 

If there is a Singularity (Vector 1,0,0), every A-Axis-Position is possible. In this case the SETANG command can define the A-Angle directly. In this case ANGTWO has no effect, because  not only 2 solutions, but also infinite solutions are possible.

 

Vector

„Angle-Position“ befor SETANG

SETANG

„Angle-Position“ after SETANG

calculated Angle-Solution

1,0,0

A0 C0

SETANG/0,0,0

A0 C0

A0 C0

1,0,0

A0 C0

SETANG/77,0,0

A77 C0

A77 C0

1,0,0

A0 C0

SETANG/-77,0,0

A-77 C0

A-77 C0

5.1     Drilling

From the Post Processor point of view are the cycles

  • NC_DRILLING
  • NC_COUNTERSINKING
  • NC_COUNTERBORING

the same. All those cycles are using the same minor word “DRILL” defined in the PP table.

5.1.1     PP Definition

 

CATIA cycle

NC_DRILLING

PP cycle

DRILL

PP syntax

CYCLE/DRILL,%MFG_TOTAL_DEPTH,%MFG_CLEAR_TIP,0,0,
%MFG_JUMP_DIST,%MFG_FEED_MACH,%MFG_SPNDL_MACH,ON,0,0,0

N1480 X85 Y35

GOTO  /   65.00000,   35.00000,   -5.00000
